***возить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:возить.html>вози́ть</a> (3723)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*voziti</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:возить.html>вози́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vozítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>abstract</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>to convey, to carry (by vehicle), to deliver, to transport</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:возить.html>Вози́ть</a></b> is an abstract verb. Its counterpart, <a href = vnd.unilang:везти.html>везти́</a>, is a concrete verb.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><i>See <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:везти.html>везти́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">veztí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> for derived verbs.</i></li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:возиться.html>вози́ться</a> (3026)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:возить.html>вози́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vozítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:возиться.html>вози́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vozítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to busy oneself, to mess around, to spend time, to take trouble
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мы.html>Нам</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:приходиться.html>прихо́дится</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:много.html>мно́го</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́тим</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:возиться.html>вози́ться</a></b>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Nam prixóditsja mnógo s étim <b>vozítʹsja</b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">We have to <b>take</b> a lot of <b>trouble</b> over this.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to tinker</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:возить.html>вози́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vozítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***возлагать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:возлагать.html>возлага́ть</a> (14978)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">воз-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">voz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-лага́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-lagátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:возлагать.html>возлага́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vozlagátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:возложить.html>возложи́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">literary</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to lay, to place <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">something on a certain area for memorial purposes</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:возлагать.html>возлага́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:цветок.html>цветы́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:могила.html>моги́лу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vozlagátʹ</b> cvetý na mogílu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to lay (or place) flowers on a grave</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">literary</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to assign <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">someone with tasks, commands, blames, hopes, or responsibilities</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:возлагать.html>возлага́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:поручение.html>поруче́ние</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> кого́-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vozlagátʹ</b> poručénije na kovó-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to entrust someone with a task</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:возлагать.html>возлага́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:командование.html>кома́ндование</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> кого́-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vozlagátʹ</b> komándovanije na kovó-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to give someone the command</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:возлагать.html>возлага́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:вино.html>вину́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> кого́-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vozlagátʹ</b> vinú na kovó-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to put the (whole) blame on someone</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:возлагать.html>возлага́ть</a></b> (<a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>все</a>) <a href = vnd.unilang:надежда.html>наде́жды</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> кого́-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vozlagátʹ</b> (vse) nadéždy na kovó-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to lay (every) one's hopes on smb.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:возлагать.html>возлага́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ответственность.html>отве́тственность</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> кого́-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vozlagátʹ</b> otvétstvennostʹ na kovó-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to make someone responsible (for something)</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***возлежавший.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:возлежать.html>возлежа́вший</a> (19605)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:возлежать.html>возлежа́вший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vozležávšij</span>)
</p>

***возложить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:возложить.html>возложи́ть</a> (11139)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">воз-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">voz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">ложи́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ložítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:возложить.html>возложи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vozložítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:возлагать.html>возлага́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">literary</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to lay, to place <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">something on a certain area for memorial purposes</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:возложить.html>возложи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:цветок.html>цветы́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:могила.html>моги́лу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vozložítʹ</b> cvetý na mogílu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to lay (or place) flowers on a grave</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">literary</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to assign <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">someone with tasks, commands, blames, hopes, or responsibilities</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:возложить.html>возложи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:поручение.html>поруче́ние</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> кого́-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vozložítʹ</b> poručénije na kovó-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to entrust someone with a task</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:возложить.html>возложи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:командование.html>кома́ндование</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> кого́-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vozložítʹ</b> komándovanije na kovó-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to give someone the command</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:возложить.html>возложи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:вино.html>вину́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> кого́-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vozložítʹ</b> vinú na kovó-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to put the (whole) blame on someone</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:возложить.html>возложи́ть</a></b> (<a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>все</a>) <a href = vnd.unilang:надежда.html>наде́жды</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> кого́-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vozložítʹ</b> (vse) nadéždy na kovó-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to lay (every) one's hopes on smb.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:возложить.html>возложи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ответственность.html>отве́тственность</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> кого́-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vozložítʹ</b> otvétstvennostʹ na kovó-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to make someone responsible (for something)</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***возлюбить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:возлюбить.html>возлюби́ть</a> (23300)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">воз-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">voz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:любить.html>люби́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ljubítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:возлюбить.html>возлюби́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vozljubítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:любить.html>люби́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">poеtic<span class="ib-comma">,</span> dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to come to love, to fall in love</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><b><a href = vnd.unilang:возлюбить.html>возлюби́ть</a></b> + кого́-либо/что́-либо (accusative case of the noun) — <b>to fall in love</b> with somebody/something, <b>to come to love</b> somebody/something</li>
<li><b><a href = vnd.unilang:возлюбить.html>возлюби́ть</a></b> + че́м-либо (instrumental case of the noun) — <b>to fall in love</b> by force of something
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:возлюбить.html>возлюби́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всем</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сердце.html>се́рдцем</a> — <i>to fall in love with all one’s heart</i></dd></dl></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:полюбить.html>полюби́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">poljubítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:возлюбленная.html>возлюбленная</a> (9658)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Feminine of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:возлюбленная.html>возлю́бленный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vozljúblennyj</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">sweetheart</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, originally a participle meaning "beloved" of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:возлюбить.html>возлюби́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vozljubítʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to love</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:возлюбленная.html>возлю́бленная</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vozljúblennaja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:возлюбленная.html>возлю́бленной</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:возлюбленная.html>возлю́бленные</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:возлюбленная.html>возлю́бленных</a></b>, <i>masculine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:возлюбленная.html>возлю́бленный</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>sweetheart</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:возмездие.html>возме́здие</a> (11596)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">воз-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">voz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мзда.html>мзда</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mzda</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ие</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:возмездие.html>возме́здие</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vozmézdije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:возмездие.html>возме́здия</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:возмездие.html>возме́здия</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:возмездие.html>возме́здий</a></b>)
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:возместить.html>возмести́ть</a> (17161)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">воз-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">voz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-мести́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-mestítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:возместить.html>возмести́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vozmestítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">возмеща́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to reimburse</li>
<li>to compensate, to indemnify, to atone <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to make reparation, compensation, or amends, for an offence or a crime</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to refund, to repay</li>
<li>to offset</li>
<li>to recoup</li>
<li>to replace</li>
<li>to redress</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:возмещение.html>возмеще́ние</a> (23401)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:возместить.html>возмести́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vozmestítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-énije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:возмещение.html>возмеще́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vozmeščénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:возмещение.html>возмеще́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:возмещение.html>возмеще́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:возмещение.html>возмеще́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>compensation, indemnification, reimbursement, refund</li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:возмутиться.html>возмути́ться</a> (4002)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:возмутить.html>возмути́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vozmutítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:возмутиться.html>возмути́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vozmutítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:возмущаться.html>возмуща́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to be indignant, to be filled with indignation, to be exasperated, to be outraged
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:возмутиться.html>возмути́ться</a></b> ке́м-либо/че́м-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vozmutítʹsja</b> kém-libo/čém-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to be indignant at/with someone/something</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to rebel</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:возмутить.html>возмути́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vozmutítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:возмущать.html>возмуща́емый</a> (18293)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:возмущаться.html>возмуща́ться</a> (6772)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:возмущать.html>возмуща́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vozmuščátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:возмущаться.html>возмуща́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vozmuščátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:возмутиться.html>возмути́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to be indignant at/with something, to be filled with indignation, to be exasperated, to be outraged</li>
<li>to rebel</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:возмущать.html>возмуща́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vozmuščátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
